 +N+Prop+Mal+Sg+Attr:@U.Cap.Obl@ # ;

LEXICON ACCRA-sur

 +N+Prop+Sur+Sg+Attr:@U.Cap.Obl@ # ;
 
LEXICON ACCRA-plc ! Place names
 +N+Prop+Plc:  ACCRADECL ;

LEXICON ACCRA-surplc ! Names that are both surnames and place names
 +N+Prop+Sur: ACCRADECL ;
 +N+Prop+Sur+Sg+Attr:@U.Cap.Obl@ # ;
 +N+Prop+Plc: ACCRADECL ;

LEXICON ACCRA ! Vowel-final names without Gradation and Ill change
 +N+Prop: ACCRADECL ;

LEXICON ACCRADECL
! These sublexica are irrelevant for ACCRA, but added
! for the sake of the lexicon MARJA
 @U.Cap.Obl@ ACCRA-DC ;
 @U.Cap.Opt@ LASJ ; 

LEXICON ACCRA-DC
 +Sg+Nom: K ;
 +Sg+Nom: R ;       
 +Ess:n K ;
 +Sg+Ill:j K ;
 +Sg+Gen: K ;
 +Sg+Gen: R ;      
 +Sg+Acc:v K ;
 +Sg+Ine:n K ;
 +Sg+Ela:s K ;
 +Pl+Nom: K ;
 +Pl+Gen:j K ;
 +Pl+Gen:j R ;     
 +Pl+Acc:jt K ;
 +Pl+Ill:jda K ;
 +Pl+Ine:jn K ;
 +Pl+Ela:js K ;
 +Pl+Com:j K ;
 +Sg+Com:X5jn K ;

LEXICON NYSTØ-OBL 
 +Sg+Nom: K ;	
 +Sg+Nom: R ;			
 +Sg+Loc:%:s K ; ! Nystø:s  !SUB
 +Sg+Gen#:a# R ; !SUB !for placenames 
 +Sg+Gen#:# R ; ! for placenames 
     NYOBL ;
 :%: NYOBL ; !SUB ! to NYOBL, optional delimiter marks. sub?
 :%- NYOBL ; !SUB
 :'1 NYOBL ; !SUB

!LEXICON NYSTØ-DC
! +laš:lažž DEARVVASLAS ;

LEXICON NYOBL
 +Sg+Nom: K ;
 +Sg+Nom: R ;        
 +Sg+Ill:j K ;
 +Ess:n K ;
 +Sg+Gen: K ;
 +Sg+Gen: R ;       
 +Sg+Acc:v K ;
 +Sg+Ine:n K ;
 +Sg+Ela:s K ;
 +Pl+Nom: K ;
 +Pl+Gen:j K ;
 +Pl+Gen:j R ;      
 +Pl+Acc:jt K ;
 +Pl+Ill:jda K ;
 +Pl+Ine:jn K ;
 +Pl+Ela:js K ;
 +Pl+Com:j K ;
 +Sg+Com:jn K ;
 +Sg+Nom:a K ;  !SUB
 +Sg+Nom:a R ;     !SUB   
 +Sg+Ill:aj K ;  !SUB
 +Ess:an K ;  !SUB
 +Sg+Gen:a K ;  !SUB
 +Sg+Gen:a R ;     !SUB  !^C^
 +Sg+Acc:av K ;   !SUB
 +Sg+Ine:an K ;  !SUB
 +Sg+Ela:as K ;  !SUB
 +Pl+Nom:a K ;   !SUB
 +Pl+Gen:aj K ;   !SUB
 +Pl+Gen:aj R ;     !SUB !^C^
 +Pl+Acc:ajt K ;   !SUB
 +Pl+Ill:ajda K ;   !SUB
 +Pl+Ine:ajn K ;   !SUB
 +Pl+Ela:ajs K ;   !SUB
 +Pl+Com:aj K ;   !SUB
 +Sg+Com:ajn K ;  !SUB

! ======================== !
! Proper name lexicon part !
! ======================== !

! A. Manually added Lule Sámi names
!    This is a intermediate solution awaiting the forthcoming
!    language-independent xml name database at gt/common/src/proper-noun.xml


! B. Dump from Northern Sámi
!    These entries are manually dumped here from propernoun-sme-lex.txt.
!    The lines from "LEXICON ProperNoun" and onwards MUST NOT be manually
!    edited, as all editions will be lost each time we dump a new version.
!    The future solution is to have a name file automatically generated 
!    from proper-noun.xml. We are not there yet.


! The present dump has no "3" in it.

LEXICON ProperNoun

! <-------- Here comes lule sami names!-->

Áj^luokta MARJA-plc ;
Stuuor^jåvrra MARJA-plc ; !sub
Skálltje MARJA-sur ;
Basudis:Basudiss HEANDARAT-plc ;
Biernna MARJA-plc ;
Bájdár:Bájddár3 DUORTNUS-plc ;
Dimbar^ásse MARJA-plc ;
Divtas^vuodna MARJA-plc ;
Divtte MARJA-plc ;
